defined_text = {
	name = GetStateName_1220
	text = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = allowrenaming_flag } }
		localization_key = STATE_1220
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { is_turkic_tag = yes }
		localization_key = STATE_1220_KIPCHAK
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				is_german_tag = yes
				AND = {
					tag = CRM
					CRM_german_colonial_administration_in_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_1220_GERMAN
	}
	text = {
		localization_key = STATE_1220
	}
}
